periodoLongo  = 21;

// CÃ¡lculo das mÃ©dias mÃ³veis

venda  = Cross(mediaLonga, mediaCurta);

// Plotar mÃ©dias no grÃ¡fico
Plot(mediaCurta, "MA Curta", colorGreen, styleLine);

09/06/2025 10:55 - Cleber Tiro Certo: // Indicador de Compra e Venda para Cripto - RSI + Candle Pattern - 1 min

// --- ParÃ¢metros ---
periodoRSI = 14;
limiteSobrevendido = 30;
limiteSobrecomprado = 70;

// --- CÃ¡lculo RSI ---
rsi = RSI(periodoRSI);

// --- IdentificaÃ§Ã£o de padrÃµes de candle simples ---

// Martelo (Hammer): corpo pequeno, sombra inferior longa
martelo = ( (High - Low) > 3 * (O - C) ) AND
          ( (C - Low) / (0.001 + High - Low) > 0.6 ) AND
          ( (O - Low) / (0.001 + High - Low) > 0.6 );

// Engolfo de Alta
engolfoAlta = ( C > O ) AND
              Ref( C, -1 ) < Ref( O, -1 ) AND
              C > Ref( O, -1 ) AND
              O < Ref( C, -1 );

// Estrela cadente (Shooting Star): corpo pequeno, sombra superior longa
estrelaCadente = ( (High - Low) > 3 * (O - C) ) AND
                 ( (High - C) / (0.001 + High - Low) > 0.6 ) AND
                 ( (High - O) / (0.001 + High - Low) > 0.6 );

// Engolfo de Baixa
engolfoBaixa = ( C < O ) AND
               Ref( C, -1 ) > Ref( O, -1 ) AND
               C < Ref( O, -1 ) AND
               O > Ref( C, -1 );

// --- LÃ³gica de Compra e Venda ---

compra = (rsi < limiteSobrevendido) AND (martelo OR engolfoAlta);
venda  = (rsi > limiteSobrecomprado) AND (estrelaCadente OR engolfoBaixa);

// --- Plot RSI em painel secundÃ¡rio ---
Plot( rsi, "RSI", colorBlue, styleLine );
Plot( limiteSobrevendido, "", colorGreen, styleDashed );
Plot( limiteSobrecomprado, "", colorRed, styleDashed );

// --- Plot Setas no grÃ¡fico de preÃ§o ---
PlotShapes( IIf(compra, shapeUpArrow, shapeNone), colorGreen, 0, Low, -20 );
PlotShapes( IIf(venda, shapeDownArrow, shapeNone), colorRed, 0, High, -20 );

// --- Plot preÃ§o normal ---
Plot( C, "PreÃ§o", colorDefault, styleCandle );

indicator("Indicador Compra/Venda - MA Crossover", overlay=true)

// ParÃ¢metros
fastLength = input.int(9, title="MÃ©dia RÃ¡pida")
slowLength = input.int(21, title="MÃ©dia Lenta")

// CÃ¡lculo das mÃ©dias
fastMA = ta.sma(close, fastLength)
slowMA = ta.sma(close, slowLength)

// Plotando

// CondiÃ§Ã£o de compra/venda

// Plotando sinais no grÃ¡fico
plotshape(buySignal, location=location.belowbar, color=color.green, style=shape.labelup, text="BUY")

09/06/2025 11:12 - Cleber Tiro Certo: //@version=5
indicator("MACD + RSI - Sinais de Compra/Venda", overlay=true)

// === ParÃ¢metros ===
macdFastLen  = input.int(12, title="MACD - MÃ©dia RÃ¡pida")
macdSlowLen  = input.int(26, title="MACD - MÃ©dia Lenta")
macdSignalLen = input.int(9, title="MACD - Linha de Sinal")
rsiLen = input.int(14, title="RSI - PerÃ­odo")
rsiOverbought = input.int(70, title="RSI - Sobrecompra")
rsiOversold   = input.int(30, title="RSI - Sobrevenda")

// === MACD ===
[macdLine, signalLine, _] = ta.macd(close, macdFastLen, macdSlowLen, macdSignalLen)
macdCrossUp   = ta.crossover(macdLine, signalLine)
macdCrossDown = ta.crossunder(macdLine, signalLine)

// === RSI ===
rsiValue = ta.rsi(close, rsiLen)
rsiBuyCondition  = rsiValue < rsiOversold
rsiSellCondition = rsiValue > rsiOverbought

// === Sinais Combinados ===
buySignal  = macdCrossUp and rsiBuyCondition
sellSignal = macdCrossDown and rsiSellCondition

# FunÃ§Ã£o que calcula sinais (exemplo simplificado)
def calcular_sinais(precos):
    # Aqui sua lÃ³gica DMI LITE real
    sinais = []
    for i in range(1, len(precos)):
        if precos[i] > precos[i-1]:
            sinais.append("compra")
        elif precos[i] < precos[i-1]:
            sinais.append("venda")
        else:
            sinais.append("manter")
    return sinais

09/06/2025 12:34 - Cleber Tiro Certo: //+------------------------------------------------------------------+
//| Expert Advisor baseado em EMAs e padrÃ£o Engulfing               |
//| Simples para compra e venda automÃ¡tica com alertas              |
//+------------------------------------------------------------------+
#property copyright "ChatGPT"
#property version   "1.0"
#property strict

// ParÃ¢metros das EMAs
input int emac_per = 3;      // EMA rÃ¡pida
input int emad_per = 13;     // EMA lenta
input int doch_time = 10;    // PerÃ­odo para suporte/resistÃªncia
input double lot_size = 0.1; // Tamanho do lote para ordens

// VariÃ¡veis globais
double EMA_fast, EMA_slow;
double EMA_fast_prev, EMA_slow_prev;

// FunÃ§Ã£o para detectar padrÃ£o Bullish Engulfing
bool IsBullishEngulfing()
{
    double open1 = iOpen(_Symbol, _Period, 1);
    double close1 = iClose(_Symbol, _Period, 1);
    double open0 = iOpen(_Symbol, _Period, 0);
    double close0 = iClose(_Symbol, _Period, 0);
    double high1 = iHigh(_Symbol, _Period, 1);
    double low1 = iLow(_Symbol, _Period, 1);
    
    return (close1 < open1) &&       // Vela anterior baixista
           (close0 > open0) &&       // Vela atual altista
           (close0 > high1) &&       // Close atual acima do high da vela anterior
           (close0 > open1);         // Close atual maior que open anterior
}

// FunÃ§Ã£o para detectar padrÃ£o Bearish Engulfing
bool IsBearishEngulfing()
{
    double open1 = iOpen(_Symbol, _Period, 1);
    double close1 = iClose(_Symbol, _Period, 1);
    double open0 = iOpen(_Symbol, _Period, 0);
    double close0 = iClose(_Symbol, _Period, 0);
    double high1 = iHigh(_Symbol, _Period, 1);
    double low1 = iLow(_Symbol, _Period, 1);

    return (close1 > open1) &&       // Vela anterior altista
           (close0 < open0) &&       // Vela atual baixista
           (close0 < low1) &&        // Close atual abaixo do low da vela anterior
           (close0 < open1);         // Close atual menor que open anterior
}

// FunÃ§Ã£o para obter suporte (mÃ­nimo nos Ãºltimos doch_time candles)
double GetSupport()
{
    double minLow = iLow(_Symbol, _Period, 0);
    for(int i=1; i<doch_time; i++)
    {
        double low = iLow(_Symbol, _Period, i);
        if(low < minLow)
            minLow = low;
    }
    return minLow;
}

// FunÃ§Ã£o para obter resistÃªncia (mÃ¡ximo nos Ãºltimos doch_time candles)
double GetResistance()
{
    double maxHigh = iHigh(_Symbol, _Period, 0);
    for(int i=1; i<doch_time; i++)
    {
        double high = iHigh(_Symbol, _Period, i);
        if(high > maxHigh)
            maxHigh = high;
    }
    return maxHigh;
}

// FunÃ§Ã£o para fechar todas posiÃ§Ãµes abertas no sÃ­mbolo atual
void CloseAllPositions()
{
    for(int i=PositionsTotal()-1; i>=0; i--)
    {
        ulong ticket = PositionGetTicket(i);
        if(PositionGetString(POSITION_SYMBOL) == _Symbol)
        {
            if(!PositionClose(ticket))
                Print("Erro ao fechar posiÃ§Ã£o ", ticket);
        }
    }
}

// FunÃ§Ã£o principal executada a cada tick
void OnTick()
{
    // Calcula EMAs rÃ¡pida e lenta
    EMA_fast = iMA(_Symbol, _Period, emac_per, 0, MODE_EMA, PRICE_TYPICAL, 0);
    EMA_slow = iMA(_Symbol, _Period, emad_per, 0, MODE_EMA, PRICE_TYPICAL, 0);
    EMA_fast_prev = iMA(_Symbol, _Period, emac_per, 0, MODE_EMA, PRICE_TYPICAL, 1);
    EMA_slow_prev = iMA(_Symbol, _Period, emad_per, 0, MODE_EMA, PRICE_TYPICAL, 1);

    // Obter suporte e resistÃªncia (apenas para exibiÃ§Ã£o)
    double suporte = GetSupport();
    double resistencia = GetResistance();

    // Cruzamento para COMPRA
    if(EMA_fast_prev < EMA_slow_prev && EMA_fast > EMA_slow)
    {
        // Fecha posiÃ§Ãµes de venda antes de comprar
        CloseAllPositions();

        // Abre ordem de COMPRA se nÃ£o tiver aberta
        if(PositionSelect(_Symbol) == false)
        {
            MqlTradeRequest request;
            MqlTradeResult result;
            request.action = TRADE_ACTION_DEAL;
            request.symbol = _Symbol;
            request.volume = lot_size;
            request.type = ORDER_TYPE_BUY;
            request.price = SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_ASK);
            request.deviation = 10;
            request.magic = 123456;
            if(!OrderSend(request, result))
                Print("Erro na ordem de COMPRA: ", GetLastError());
            else
                Print("Ordem de COMPRA aberta com sucesso");
        }
        Alert("Cruzamento de EMAs para COMPRA");
    }

    // Cruzamento para VENDA
    if(EMA_fast_prev > EMA_slow_prev && EMA_fast < EMA_slow)
    {
        // Fecha posiÃ§Ãµes de compra antes de vender
        CloseAllPositions();

        // Abre ordem de VENDA se nÃ£o tiver aberta
        if(PositionSelect(_Symbol) == false)
        {
            MqlTradeRequest request;
            MqlTradeResult result;
            request.action = TRADE_ACTION_DEAL;
            request.symbol = _Symbol;
            request.volume = lot_size;
            request.type = ORDER_TYPE_SELL;
            request.price = SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_BID);
            request.deviation = 10;
            request.magic = 123456;
            if(!OrderSend(request, result))
                Print("Erro na ordem de VENDA: ", GetLastError());
            else
                Print("Ordem de VENDA aberta com sucesso");
        }
        Alert("Cruzamento de EMAs para VENDA");
    }

    // Detecta padrÃ£o Bullish Engulfing
    if(IsBullishEngulfing())
    {
        CloseAllPositions();
        if(PositionSelect(_Symbol) == false)
        {
            MqlTradeRequest request;
            MqlTradeResult result;
            request.action = TRADE_ACTION_DEAL;
            request.symbol = _Symbol;
            request.volume = lot_size;
            request.type = ORDER_TYPE_BUY;
            request.price = SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_ASK);
            request.deviation = 10;
            request.magic = 123456;
            if(!OrderSend(request, result))
                Print("Erro na ordem de COMPRA Bullish Engulfing: ", GetLastError());
            else
                Print("Ordem de COMPRA Bullish Engulfing aberta");
        }
        Alert("Sinal de Compra: Bullish Engulfing");
    }

    // Detecta padrÃ£o Bearish Engulfing
    if(IsBearishEngulfing())
    {
        CloseAllPositions();
        if(PositionSelect(_Symbol) == false)
        {
            MqlTradeRequest request;
            MqlTradeResult result;
            request.action = TRADE_ACTION_DEAL;
            request.symbol = _Symbol;

            request.type = ORDER_TYPE_SELL;

                Print("Erro na ordem de VENDA Bearish Engulfing: ", GetLastError());
            else
                Print("Ordem de VENDA Bearish Engulfing aberta");
        }

    }
}

//| Expert Advisor baseado em EMAs e padrÃ£o Engulfing               |

//+------------------------------------------------------------------+
#property copyright "ChatGPT"

// ParÃ¢metros das EMAs
input int emac_per = 3;      // EMA rÃ¡pida

input int tp_points = 150;          // Take Profit em pontos

           (close0 > open0) &&       // Vela atual altista
           (close0 > high1) &&       // Close atual acima do high da vela anterior

    double close0 = iClose(_Symbol, _Period, 0);
    double low1 = iLow(_Symbol, _Period, 1);

           (close0 < open1);         // Close atual menor que open anterior

// FunÃ§Ã£o para obter suporte (mÃ­nimo nos Ãºltimos doch_time candles)
double GetSupport()

    for(int i=1; i<doch_time; i++)
    {

// FunÃ§Ã£o para fechar todas posiÃ§Ãµes abertas no sÃ­mbolo atual
void CloseAllPositions()
{
    for(int i=PositionsTotal()-1; i>=0; i--)
    {
        ulong ticket = PositionGetTicket(i);
        if(PositionGetString(POSITION_SYMBOL) == _Symbol)
        {
            if(!PositionClose(ticket))
                Print("Erro ao fechar posiÃ§Ã£o ", ticket);
        }
    }
}

// FunÃ§Ã£o para abrir ordem com SL e TP
bool OpenOrder(int order_type)
{
    MqlTradeRequest request;
    MqlTradeResult result;

    double price = 0;
    double sl = 0;
    double tp = 0;
    double point = SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_POINT);

    if(order_type == ORDER_TYPE_BUY)
    {
        price = SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_ASK);
        sl = price - sl_points * point;
        tp = price + tp_points * point;
    }
    else if(order_type == ORDER_TYPE_SELL)
    {
        price = SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_BID);
        sl = price + sl_points * point;
        tp = price - tp_points * point;
    }
    else
        return false;

    request.action = TRADE_ACTION_DEAL;
    request.symbol = _Symbol;
    request.volume = lot_size;
    request.type = order_type;
    request.price = price;
    request.sl = sl;
    request.tp = tp;
    request.deviation = 10;
    request.magic = 123456;

    if(!OrderSend(request, result))
    {
        Print("Erro ao abrir ordem: ", GetLastError());
        return false;
    }
    else
    {
        Print("Ordem aberta com sucesso, tipo: ", order_type == ORDER_TYPE_BUY ? "COMPRA" : "VENDA");
        return true;
    }
}

// FunÃ§Ã£o principal executada a cada tick
void OnTick()
{
    EMA_fast = iMA(_Symbol, _Period, emac_per, 0, MODE_EMA, PRICE_TYPICAL, 0);
    EMA_slow = iMA(_Symbol, _Period, emad_per, 0, MODE_EMA, PRICE_TYPICAL, 0);
    EMA_fast_prev = iMA(_Symbol, _Period, emac_per, 0, MODE_EMA, PRICE_TYPICAL, 1);
    EMA_slow_prev = iMA(_Symbol, _Period, emad_per, 0, MODE_EMA, PRICE_TYPICAL, 1);

    // Cruzamento para COMPRA
    if(EMA_fast_prev < EMA_slow_prev && EMA_fast > EMA_slow)
    {
        CloseAllPositions();
        if(PositionSelect(_Symbol) == false)
        {
            if(OpenOrder(ORDER_TYPE_BUY))
                Alert("Cruzamento de EMAs para COMPRA");
        }
    }

    // Cruzamento para VENDA
    if(EMA_fast_prev > EMA_slow_prev && EMA_fast < EMA_slow)
    {
        CloseAllPositions();
        if(PositionSelect(_Symbol) == false)
        {
            if(OpenOrder(ORDER_TYPE_SELL))
                Alert("Cruzamento de EMAs para VENDA");
        }
    }

    // Detecta padrÃ£o Bullish Engulfing
    if(IsBullishEngulfing())
    {
        CloseAllPositions();
        if(PositionSelect(_Symbol) == false)
        {
            if(OpenOrder(ORDER_TYPE_BUY))
                Alert("Sinal de Compra: Bullish Engulfing");
        }
    }

    // Detecta padrÃ£o Bearish Engulfing
    if(IsBearishEngulfing())
    {
        CloseAllPositions();
        if(PositionSelect(_Symbol) == false)
        {
            if(OpenOrder(ORDER_TYPE_SELL))
                Alert("Sinal de Venda: Bearish Engulfing");
        }
    }
}

#property copyright "Seu Nome"

input int    FastEMAPeriod = 3;
input int    SlowEMAPeriod = 13;
input int    MicroTrendPeriod = 10;
input int    MacroTrendPeriod = 100;
input double Lots = 0.1;
input double StopLoss = 100;
input double TakeProfit = 200;

//+------------------------------------------------------------------+
//| Expert initialization function                                   |
//+------------------------------------------------------------------+

  {
   return(INIT_SUCCEEDED);
  }

//| Expert deinitialization function                                 |
//+------------------------------------------------------------------+

  {
   
  }
//+------------------------------------------------------------------+
//| Expert tick function                                             |
//+------------------------------------------------------------------+
void OnTick()
  {
   double FastEMA = iMA(NULL, 0, FastEMAPeriod, 0, MODE_EMA, PRICE_TYPICAL, 0);
   double FastEMA_prev = iMA(NULL, 0, FastEMAPeriod, 0, MODE_EMA, PRICE_TYPICAL, 1);
   
   double SlowEMA = iMA(NULL, 0, SlowEMAPeriod, 0, MODE_EMA, PRICE_TYPICAL, 0);
   double SlowEMA_prev = iMA(NULL, 0, SlowEMAPeriod, 0, MODE_EMA, PRICE_TYPICAL, 1);
   
   // Engulfing candle bullish
   bool BullishEngulfing = (Close[1] < Open[1]) && (Close[0] > Open[0]) && (Close[0] > High[1]) && (Close[2] >= Open[0]);
   
   // Engulfing candle bearish
   bool BearishEngulfing = (Close[1] > Open[1]) && (Close[0] < Open[0]) && (Close[0] < Low[1]) && (Close[2] <= Open[0]);

   // Check for bullish entry
   if(FastEMA_prev < SlowEMA_prev && FastEMA > SlowEMA && BullishEngulfing && PositionsTotal() == 0)
     {
      // Send BUY order
      double Ask = SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_ASK);
      double sl = Ask - StopLoss * _Point;
      double tp = Ask + TakeProfit * _Point;
      
      OrderSend(_Symbol, OP_BUY, Lots, Ask, 3, sl, tp, "EMA Engulfing BUY", 0, 0, clrGreen);
     }

   // Check for bearish entry
   if(FastEMA_prev > SlowEMA_prev && FastEMA < SlowEMA && BearishEngulfing && PositionsTotal() == 0)
     {
      // Send SELL order
      double Bid = SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_BID);
      double sl = Bid + StopLoss * _Point;
      double tp = Bid - TakeProfit * _Point;
      
      OrderSend(_Symbol, OP_SELL, Lots, Bid, 3, sl, tp, "EMA Engulfing SELL", 0, 0, clrRed);
     }
  }

//|                                                EMA_Engulfing_Moderado_EA.mq5 |

#property copyright "Seu Nome"

input int    FastEMAPeriod = 3;
input int    SlowEMAPeriod = 13;

input int    MacroTrendPeriod = 100;
input double Lots = 0.1;
input double StopLoss = 100;
input double TakeProfit = 200;
input int    CooldownCandles = 10; // NÂº de candles de espera apÃ³s entrada

datetime LastTradeTime = 0;

//+------------------------------------------------------------------+
//| Expert initialization function                                   |
//+------------------------------------------------------------------+
int OnInit()
  {
   return(INIT_SUCCEEDED);
  }
//+------------------------------------------------------------------+
//| Expert deinitialization function                                 |
//+------------------------------------------------------------------+

  {
   
  }
//+------------------------------------------------------------------+
//| Expert tick function                                             |
//+------------------------------------------------------------------+
void OnTick()
  {
   double FastEMA = iMA(NULL, 0, FastEMAPeriod, 0, MODE_EMA, PRICE_TYPICAL, 0);
   double FastEMA_prev = iMA(NULL, 0, FastEMAPeriod, 0, MODE_EMA, PRICE_TYPICAL, 1);
   
   double SlowEMA = iMA(NULL, 0, SlowEMAPeriod, 0, MODE_EMA, PRICE_TYPICAL, 0);
   double SlowEMA_prev = iMA(NULL, 0, SlowEMAPeriod, 0, MODE_EMA, PRICE_TYPICAL, 1);
   
   // Engulfing candle bullish
   bool BullishEngulfing = (Close[1] < Open[1]) && (Close[0] > Open[0]) && (Close[0] > High[1]) && (Close[2] >= Open[0]);
   
   // Engulfing candle bearish
   bool BearishEngulfing = (Close[1] > Open[1]) && (Close[0] < Open[0]) && (Close[0] < Low[1]) && (Close[2] <= Open[0]);

   // ProteÃ§Ã£o de "cooldown" (espera entre trades)
   int current_bar_time = (int)Time[0];
   if(LastTradeTime != 0 && (current_bar_time - LastTradeTime) < (CooldownCandles * PeriodSeconds()))
     return; // Ainda em cooldown

   // Check for bullish entry
   if(FastEMA_prev < SlowEMA_prev && FastEMA > SlowEMA && BullishEngulfing && PositionsTotal() == 0)
     {
      // Send BUY order
      double Ask = SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_ASK);
      double sl = Ask - StopLoss * _Point;
      double tp = Ask + TakeProfit * _Point;
      
      if(OrderSend(_Symbol, OP_BUY, Lots, Ask, 3, sl, tp, "EMA Engulfing BUY", 0, 0, clrGreen) > 0)
        LastTradeTime = current_bar_time;
     }

   // Check for bearish entry
   if(FastEMA_prev > SlowEMA_prev && FastEMA < SlowEMA && BearishEngulfing && PositionsTotal() == 0)
     {
      // Send SELL order
      double Bid = SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_BID);
      double sl = Bid + StopLoss * _Point;
      double tp = Bid - TakeProfit * _Point;
      
      if(OrderSend(_Symbol, OP_SELL, Lots, Bid, 3, sl, tp, "EMA Engulfing SELL", 0, 0, clrRed) > 0)
        LastTradeTime = current_bar_time;
     }
  }

09/06/2025 13:31 - Cleber Tiro Certo: *CÃ³digo do ROBÃ” TIRO CERTO para MT5:*ğŸ‘‡
09/06/2025 13:31 - Cleber Tiro Certo: //+------------------------------------------------------------------+
//|                                                   RoboTiroCerto.mq5|
//|                     Desenvolvido para vocÃª                       |
//+------------------------------------------------------------------+
#property copyright "ChatGPT"
#property version   "1.0"
#property strict

input int EMAMicroPeriod = 10;           // PerÃ­odo EMA micro tendÃªncia
input int EMAMacroPeriod = 100;          // PerÃ­odo EMA macro tendÃªncia
input int EMARapidaPeriod = 3;           // EMA rÃ¡pida para cruzamento
input int EMALentaPeriod = 13;           // EMA lenta para cruzamento

input double RiskMinPercent = 3.0;       // Risco mÃ­nimo (% do saldo)
input double RiskMaxPercent = 10.0;      // Risco mÃ¡ximo (% do saldo)

input ENUM_TIMEFRAMES OperateTimeframe = PERIOD_M5;  // Timeframe para operar
input double StopLossPips = 30;           // Stop Loss em pips padrÃ£o
input double TakeProfitPips = 60;         // Take Profit em pips padrÃ£o

//--- VariÃ¡veis globais
double LotSize = 0.0;

//+------------------------------------------------------------------+
//| FunÃ§Ã£o para calcular o lote baseado no risco e StopLoss         |
//+------------------------------------------------------------------+
double CalculateLotSize(double risk_percent, double stoploss_pips)
  {
   double balance = AccountInfoDouble(ACCOUNT_BALANCE);
   double risk_money = balance * (risk_percent / 100.0);
   double tick_value = SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_TRADE_TICK_VALUE);
   double tick_size = SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_TRADE_TICK_SIZE);
   double point = SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_POINT);

   if(tick_value == 0 || tick_size == 0)
     return(0);

   // Valor por ponto de movimento no lote 1
   double lot_step = SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_VOLUME_STEP);
   double min_lot = SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_VOLUME_MIN);
   double max_lot = SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_VOLUME_MAX);

   // Calculo de pips baseado em pontos (exemplo: 1 pip = 10 pontos para forex)
   double pip_value = stoploss_pips * point;

   // Lote = risco dinheiro / (stoploss pips * valor do pip por lote 1)
   double lot = risk_money / (stoploss_pips * tick_value / tick_size);

   // Ajustar lote para passo e limites da corretora
   lot = MathMax(lot, min_lot);
   lot = MathMin(lot, max_lot);
   lot = MathFloor(lot / lot_step) * lot_step;

   return(lot);
  }

//+------------------------------------------------------------------+
//| FunÃ§Ã£o para determinar cenÃ¡rio e definir risco adaptativo       |
//+------------------------------------------------------------------+
double GetAdaptiveRisk()
  {
   // Vamos avaliar com base na forÃ§a das EMAs micro e macro tendÃªncia
   double EMA_Micro = iMA(_Symbol, OperateTimeframe, EMAMicroPeriod, 0, MODE_EMA, PRICE_CLOSE, 0);
   double EMA_Micro_Previous = iMA(_Symbol, OperateTimeframe, EMAMicroPeriod, 0, MODE_EMA, PRICE_CLOSE, 1);
   double EMA_Macro = iMA(_Symbol, OperateTimeframe, EMAMacroPeriod, 0, MODE_EMA, PRICE_CLOSE, 0);
   double EMA_Macro_Previous = iMA(_Symbol, OperateTimeframe, EMAMacroPeriod, 0, MODE_EMA, PRICE_CLOSE, 1);

   double atr = iATR(_Symbol, OperateTimeframe, 14, 0);

   bool strongUpTrend = (EMA_Micro > EMA_Micro_Previous) && (EMA_Micro > EMA_Macro);
   bool strongDownTrend = (EMA_Micro < EMA_Micro_Previous) && (EMA_Micro < EMA_Macro);

   double volatility = atr / SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_POINT);

   // DefiniÃ§Ã£o simples do risco adaptativo
   if(strongUpTrend || strongDownTrend)
     {
      if(volatility < 50)  // Baixa volatilidade = maior confianÃ§a
        return RiskMaxPercent;
      else if(volatility < 100)
        return (RiskMinPercent + RiskMaxPercent) / 2;
      else
        return RiskMinPercent;
     }
   else
     return RiskMinPercent;
  }

//+------------------------------------------------------------------+
//| FunÃ§Ã£o para detectar padrÃ£o Engulfing para compra                |
//+------------------------------------------------------------------+
bool IsBullEngulfing()
  {
   double open1 = iOpen(_Symbol, OperateTimeframe, 1);
   double close1 = iClose(_Symbol, OperateTimeframe, 1);
   double open2 = iOpen(_Symbol, OperateTimeframe, 2);
   double close2 = iClose(_Symbol, OperateTimeframe, 2);
   double high2 = iHigh(_Symbol, OperateTimeframe, 2);

   return (close2 < open2) && (close1 > open1) && (close1 > high2);
  }

//+------------------------------------------------------------------+
//| FunÃ§Ã£o para detectar padrÃ£o Engulfing para venda                 |
//+------------------------------------------------------------------+
bool IsBearEngulfing()
  {
   double open1 = iOpen(_Symbol, OperateTimeframe, 1);
   double close1 = iClose(_Symbol, OperateTimeframe, 1);
   double open2 = iOpen(_Symbol, OperateTimeframe, 2);
   double close2 = iClose(_Symbol, OperateTimeframe, 2);
   double low2 = iLow(_Symbol, OperateTimeframe, 2);

   return (close2 > open2) && (close1 < open1) && (close1 < low2);
  }

//+------------------------------------------------------------------+
//| FunÃ§Ã£o principal OnTick                                          |
//+------------------------------------------------------------------+
void OnTick()
  {
   static bool positionOpen = false;
   static ulong ticket = 0;

   double EMA_Rapida_Previous = iMA(_Symbol, OperateTimeframe, EMARapidaPeriod, 0, MODE_EMA, PRICE_CLOSE, 1);
   double EMA_Lenta_Previous = iMA(_Symbol, OperateTimeframe, EMALentaPeriod, 0, MODE_EMA, PRICE_CLOSE, 1);
   double EMA_Rapida_Current = iMA(_Symbol, OperateTimeframe, EMARapidaPeriod, 0, MODE_EMA, PRICE_CLOSE, 0);
   double EMA_Lenta_Current = iMA(_Symbol, OperateTimeframe, EMALentaPeriod, 0, MODE_EMA, PRICE_CLOSE, 0);

   // Detecta cruzamento de EMAs
   bool cruzouParaCima = (EMA_Rapida_Previous < EMA_Lenta_Previous) && (EMA_Rapida_Current > EMA_Lenta_Current);
   bool cruzouParaBaixo = (EMA_Rapida_Previous > EMA_Lenta_Previous) && (EMA_Rapida_Current < EMA_Lenta_Current);

   // Define risco adaptativo e calcula lote
   double riscoAtual = GetAdaptiveRisk();
   double loteAtual = CalculateLotSize(riscoAtual, StopLossPips);

   // Se jÃ¡ existe posiÃ§Ã£o aberta, nÃ£o abrir outra
   if(PositionSelect(_Symbol))
     {
      // Pode implementar lÃ³gica para gerenciar posiÃ§Ãµes (trailing stop, TP parcial etc)
      return;
     }

   // Entradas de compra
   if(cruzouParaCima && IsBullEngulfing())
     {
      MqlTradeRequest request;
      MqlTradeResult result;
      ZeroMemory(request);
      ZeroMemory(result);

      request.action = TRADE_ACTION_DEAL;
      request.symbol = _Symbol;
      request.volume = loteAtual;
      request.type = ORDER_TYPE_BUY;
      request.price = SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_ASK);
      request.sl = request.price - StopLossPips * SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_POINT);
      request.tp = request.price + TakeProfitPips * SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_POINT);
      request.deviation = 10;
      request.magic = 123456;
      request.comment = "ROBÃ” TIRO CERTO - COMPRA";

      if(!OrderSend(request,result))
         Print("Erro ordem compra: ", GetLastError());
      else
         Print("Ordem compra enviada: lote ", loteAtual);
     }

   // Entradas de venda
   if(cruzouParaBaixo && IsBearEngulfing())
     {
      MqlTradeRequest request;
      MqlTradeResult result;
      ZeroMemory(request);
      ZeroMemory(result);

      request.action = TRADE_ACTION_DEAL;
      request.symbol = _Symbol;
      request.volume = loteAtual;
      request.type = ORDER_TYPE_SELL;
      request.price = SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_BID);
      request.sl = request.price + StopLossPips * SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_POINT);
      request.tp = request.price - TakeProfitPips * SymbolInfoDouble(_Symbol, SYMBOL_POINT);
      request.deviation = 10;
      request.magic = 123456;
      request.comment = "ROBÃ” TIRO CERTO - VENDA";

      if(!OrderSend(request,result))
         Print("Erro ordem venda: ", GetLastError());
      else
         Print("Ordem venda enviada: lote ", loteAtual);
     }
  }
